<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Scotch tape</i>, but the meaning has expanded beyond the corresponding meaning in English.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>adhesive tape</li></ol>

<p><b>ско́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-кош-</b>; суффикс: <b>-енн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрашивать.html>скра́шивать</a> (29092)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">скра́сить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrásitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрашивать.html>скра́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrášivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">скра́сить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soften, to mitigate (something painful)</li>
<li>to brighten, to make more attractive (something dull or boring)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепить.html>крепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fasten <i>(together)</i>, to pin <i>(together)</i>, to tie, to clamp, to bolt, to mortar</li>
<li>to strengthen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>скрепя́</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepjá</b> sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reluctantly; grudgingly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seal, to sign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́тью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepítʹ</b> dokumént pečátʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attach a seal to the document</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepítʹ</b> pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sign; fix one's signature</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepítʹ</b> vtorój pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to countersign</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скреплённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljónnyj</b> króvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sealed with blood (friendship etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скреплённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrepljónnyj</span>)
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>скреп<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лён<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/b(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-крепл-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ённ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***скреплять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a> (25919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrepljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fasten <i>(together)</i>, to pin <i>(together)</i>, to tie, to clamp, to bolt, to mortar</li>
<li>to strengthen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>скрепя́</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepjá</b> sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reluctantly; grudgingly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seal, to sign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́тью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljátʹ</b> dokumént pečátʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attach a seal to the document</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljátʹ</b> pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sign; fix one's signature</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljátʹ</b> vtorój pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to countersign</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скреплённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljónnyj</b> króvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sealed with blood (friendship etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>скреп<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a>.

***скрести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́</a> (12899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skresti</i>, cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">скребти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrebtý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">скрэ́бці</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrébci</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skripétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскрипеть.html>проскрипе́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипнуть.html>скри́пнуть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скроить.html>скрои́ть</a> (12621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kroítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скроить.html>скрои́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skroítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кроить.html>крои́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut out (fabric to specific lengths and shapes to make clothes)</li></ol>
